2013-05-15 17:43:43
Bhavesh Bhatia
199538
3.5
DELIGHTFUL AND CHEAP FOOD!

In the heart of Kolkata, a dinghy lane leads you to a small Chinese eatery called Tibetan Delight. Don't be fooled by its name as it serves both Chinese and Tibetan fare. Like many Chinese restaurants in Tangra, Tibetan Delight on Chowringhee Road also has a loyal clientele for its authentic and tasty Chinese food. It is a small eatery that serves up brilliant food with efficient service.

This is one food joint in Kolkata that serves not only good but cheap and stomach filling Chinese food. The small establishment is best known for their fiery Chinese dishes. They are synonymous for their momos. Whether pan-fried or steamed, their momo's are always delicious and come in generous portions.  Once there, you can try their pan-fried chicken momo's with golden fried prawns and chicken satay. For the main course sample their Mongolian fried rice with Manchurian fish. If rice is not your thing then I would recommend their Non Veg Chilli Garlic noodles and other Hakka noodle dishes. Otherwise, try their Chicken Lollipops which are considered by many to be the house best seller. Some other unforgettable Chinese items to be had here are Chilli Chicken (dry), Sichuan Chicken and the two kinds of pepper chicken. Both versions of pepper chicken are full of flavor; one version is with the sweet and spicy sauce while the other is like fried chicken strips. Chilli Roast Pork is considered by many to be one of their signature dishes; I really liked it. The meat pieces are well cut and are presented in gravy of onion, chillies and capsicum. This is not the usual chilli pork roast that is found in many Chinese food joints. 

At times, the food quality of certain items might suffer but this is definitely a place that will continue to have takers for its cheap and tasty Chinese delicacies.

##

2013-01-28 18:31:21
Nikhil Kajaria
207975
4.5
This is a small, dainty little place near the Exide crossing. Finding it is also a task in itself as it's located in a narrow gully that sits between a row of shops. However, once there, you will not regret the effort as they are, quite easily, one of the best Tibetan joints in the city. The Momos are delicious, served with Chilli Sauce that is a little too spicy. The prices are very reasonable and the service is quick and efficient.

The only real negative is that the stock for cold drinks is limited so whenever you need that extra drink after all that Chilli, you might just find yourself in bad luck.

2012-10-24 21:01:47
Rahul Ganguly
338227
4.0
Had some wonderful times here during my college years. Easy on the pocket, this little place has its charm. The entrance alone, replete with twinkling lights and prayer flags, sets the stage for the quaint eatery. Try their pan fired momos and the chili garlic noodles - unforgettable stuff of legends, done inimitably in the old-Calcutta style. This is Tibetan cooking with a distinct Hakka touch, and the result is magic on your taste buds. Highly recommended!

##

2012-10-18 17:03:36
Anirban Raychaudhury
348287
4.0
A bit difficult to find out, the ambiance may put you down but wait till the dishes come to your table. Must try- roasted chilly pork, garlic chicken, the mixed fried rice and pork momos. An excellent value for money place. One of the oldest places to serve momo in kolkata, i guess it dates back to 1960's. It would seat about 16 people together, on weekends you might have to wait for an hour to get a place. 2 portions of rice/noodles, 1 starter ,  1 side dish would cost you around 300. A little info for the first time goers- the restaurant is located on 2 feet wide lane beside laxmi chand babu ka asli sone ka dukan( the dukan which is adjacent to the road leading to momo plaza or the backside of sambhunath pandit hospital), gather some strength and walk straight in you will find the place.

2012-10-07 22:29:58
Shreyasee Gupta
167883
4.0
The reason i chose to give it four stars is because it manages to fill hungry stomachs without pinching the pocket and leaves the taste buds happy and satisfied-which is no mean feat. 
The best thing about Tibetan delight if you ask me are the spicy chinese dishes it serves-from the non veg chilli garlic noodles,to the chilli chicken dry and the pepper chicken(incidentally i have been served two versions of pepper chicken from this same place-one which was awesome cooked in the perfect sweet and spicy sauce and the other,well forgettable-just fried chicken strips,nothing special..so before you order make sure you ask which one they have on offer).
I also had momos here..Both fried as well as the Pan fried versions(am not a great fan of steamed momos)..While the fried momos were okay,the pan fried momos were just steamed momos cooked in some sweet sauce which i didnt like(if you really want to have momos head next door to Momo Plaza)..
P.S.Once you're done with all the fiery chinese food,wash it down with chilled Thums Up or Coke and you'll feel yourself up on Cloud Nine..

fried rice- makes you regret for ordering it after a moment

the alley leading to tibetan delight is very dingy and narrow which makes this place very hard to be discovered.
overall its a place that lacks consistency in their quality. sometimes its good and sometimes it makes u feel like having utterly cheap quality food and hence it might not make you visit this place again!

##

2012-09-27 13:31:36
Debanjan Bose
307985
4.0
I'd have given 3 stars, but it deserves 4 for the amount of times it has satiated the immense belly needs and with such good quality and low price. In short, I love this place.

Pork/Chicken Steamed Momo - Probably one of the most 'cheapest-but-tastiest' things in the city. Generous size of the momo shall also make you happy. Interestingly, their momo soup has rather been evolving and tastes quite good now - unlike the blandness I use to face back in the day.

Pork Roast - This is specially for the lovers of the animal. Slender, well cut pieces (with or without fat) comes in this crazy, not dominatiing, gravy of onions, chillies and capsicum. This is not your usual Pork Chilly. You'll be left asking for more. Guraranteed.

Chk. Garlic Noodles - The much loved fare is cooked to perfection. Although there were instances of it being a little burnt, but funnily that added to the taste.

Their Tibetan fare is quite nice. I do not completely recollect my thoughts after having food their most of the times. But, I have never come out disappointed and with a very light wallet. Now, that is food.

Finding it is usually a problem for first timers. The goli just comes from nowhere and is quite sharp on your left as you walk on the pavement that leads to Elgin Road. However, once found you'll never forget it. It is also away from the hustle of the main road.

The problem is space. I have had to wait on numerous occasions. they just have 4 tables, which will seat 4 people (a one of two extra on one table maybe). Instead, they also spread table outside the eatery in a little open space. However, the wait is worthy of the act. 

If you have not been here, you are missing something.
